      function is_ie() {
      				var ua = window.navigator.userAgent; //Check the userAgent property of the window.navigator object
      				var msie = ua.indexOf('MSIE '); // IE 10 or older
      				var trident = ua.indexOf('Trident/'); //IE 11

      				return (msie > 0 || trident > 0);
      			}

      			function not_excluded_page() {
      				return (window.location.href.indexOf("/unsupported-browser/") === - 1 && document.title.toLowerCase().indexOf('page not found') === - 1);
      			}

      			if (is_ie() && not_excluded_page()) {
      				window.location = location.protocol + '//' + location.host + '/unsupported-browser/';
      			}

                    <h3 id="p-694144301fa52-title" class="h3 b-news__first-title">
                      <span>
                        New hope for a hard-to-treat lung cancer
                      </span>
                    </h3>
                    <p class="p b-news__first-excerpt">
                      Sevabertinib, created by the Broad-Bayer oncology research alliance, is a new oral treatment option for a type of non-small-cell lung cancer, the most common type of lung cancer.
                    </p>
                    <a class="b-news__first-cta is-target-link" id="p-694144301fa52-link" aria-labelledby="p-694144301fa52-title" aria-describedby="p-694144301fa52-link" data-js="target-link" href="https://www.broadinstitute.org/news/fda-approves-first-cancer-drug-based-broad-institute-science">

          <section class=" c-block b-columns t-theme--light">
            <div class="l-container b-columns__container">
              <header class="c-block__content-block c-block__header b-columns__header c-content-block c-content-block--layout-left">
                <h2 class="c-block__title b-columns__title h3 c-content-block__title">
                  Pushing scholarship ahead
                </h2>
                <div class="c-content-block__content-wrap">
                  <div class="c-block__description b-columns__description t-sink s-sink c-content-block__content">
                    <p>
                      Throughout the humanities, breakthroughs and discoveries change the way we see the world and inform the way we improve it.
                    </p>
                  </div>
                  <p class="c-content-block__cta">
                    <a class="c-block__cta-link a-btn a-btn-secondary a-btn--arrow-right  c-content-block__cta-link" href="https://news.harvard.edu/gazette/story/2025/05/hooking-first-years-on-the-arts-and-humanities/" aria-label="Learn more about how Harvard is innovating scholarship">
                      <span class="a-btn__text">
                        Learn more about how Harvard is innovating scholarship
                      </span>
                    </a>
                  </p>
                </div>
              </header>
              <div class="b-columns__list b-columns__row b-columns--count-4">
                <div class="b-columns__col">
                  <div class="b-columns__col-content t-sink s-sink">
                    <figure class="wp-image wp-image--no-caption alignnone">
                      <img decoding="async" style="margin-top:-10px; margin-bottom:-10px;" src="https://www.harvard.edu/wp-content/uploads/2025/12/EvansHughes2.jpg" alt="two people on an archeological dig">
                    </figure>
                    <h3 style="margin-top:-10px;" class="h-default is-style-h4">
                      Understanding the Earth
                    </h3>
                    <p>
                      Through research and archeology, Harvard scientists got one step closer to
                      <a href="https://news.harvard.edu/gazette/story/2025/07/a-step-toward-solving-central-mystery-of-life-on-earth/">
                        understanding the origins of life
                      </a>
                      and the early history of
                      <a href="https://news.harvard.edu/gazette/story/newsplus/fossil-discovery-uncovers-early-history-of-earths-largest-animal-group/">
                        Earths largest animal group
                      </a>
                      .
                    </p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div class="b-columns__col">
                  <div class="b-columns__col-content t-sink s-sink">
                    <figure class="wp-image wp-image--no-caption alignnone">
                      <img decoding="async" style="margin-top:-10px; margin-bottom:-10px;" src="https://www.harvard.edu/wp-content/uploads/2025/12/Han-Article-Banner-Image.jpg" alt="An illustration showing a black hole within a cloud in space">
                    </figure>
                    <h3 style="margin-top:-10px;" class="h-default is-style-h4">
                      Exploring the stars
                    </h3>
                    <p>
                      Research papers from Harvard astronomers explored new evidence of the
                      <a href="https://gsas.harvard.edu/news/massive-discovery">
                        closest known supermassive black hole
                      </a>
                      and a cosmic explosion that could be a rare flare from a magnetar
                      <a href="https://chandra.harvard.edu/press/25_releases/press_022525.html">
                        one of the most mysterious objects in the universe
                      </a>
                      .
                    </p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div class="b-columns__col">
                  <div class="b-columns__col-content t-sink s-sink">
                    <figure class="wp-image wp-image--no-caption alignnone">
                      <img decoding="async" style="margin-top:-10px; margin-bottom:-10px;" src="https://www.harvard.edu/wp-content/uploads/2025/12/macarthur_Math_1920.jpg" alt="Lauren Williams teaching">
                    </figure>
                    <h3 style="margin-top:-10px;" class="h-default is-style-h4">
                      Crunching the numbers
                    </h3>
                    <p>
                      Harvards
                      <a href="https://news.harvard.edu/gazette/story/2025/10/lauren-williams-awarded-macarthur-genius-grant/">
                        Lauren Williams won a MacArthur genius grant
                      </a>
                      for her theoretical breakthroughs understanding phenomena such as tsunamis and traffic.
                    </p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div class="b-columns__col">
                  <div class="b-columns__col-content t-sink s-sink">
                    <figure class="wp-image wp-image--no-caption alignnone">
                      <img decoding="async" style="margin-top:-10px; margin-bottom:-10px;" src="https://www.harvard.edu/wp-content/uploads/2025/12/AdobeStock_460866760b.jpg" alt="A plane flying over green land">
                    </figure>
                    <h3 style="margin-top:-10px;" class="h-default is-style-h4">
                      Protecting the planet
                    </h3>
                    <p>
                      Harvard researchers are learning how to
                      <a href="https://news.harvard.edu/gazette/story/2025/09/seeking-a-carbon-capture-breakthrough/">
                        capture emissions from fuels
                      </a>
                      and create
                      <a href="https://seas.harvard.edu/news/2025/11/next-frontier-clean-flight-jet-fuel-city-waste">
                        fuels from renewable sources
                      </a>
                      , like city waste.
                    </p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </section>
          <section class=" c-block b-header t-theme--light">
            <div class="l-container b-header__container">
              <header class="c-block__content-block c-block__header b-header__header c-content-block c-content-block--layout-left">
                <h2 class="c-block__title b-header__title h3 c-content-block__title">
                  The next generation
                </h2>
                <div class="c-content-block__content-wrap">
                  <div class="c-block__description b-header__description t-sink s-sink c-content-block__content">
                    <p>
                      Harvards strong history of mentorship is guiding this years students to uncovering next years breakthroughs.
                    </p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </header>
              <hr class="b-header__border">
            </div>
          </section>
